# Context — Master Index

This folder is the project's persistent memory, organised as a **context
tree** (fractal book metaphor):

```
context/
├── MASTER.md          ← the contents page (you are here)
├── prior research/    ← chapter files mapping `02` and `03` codebases
└── *.md               ← future top-level chapter files
```

`MASTER.md` is the table of contents. Every chapter on the shelf gets a row
here with a one-line summary. Each chapter is its own markdown file that
goes deep on a single topic.

---

## How it works

### Reading (recall)
1. Open `MASTER.md` (this file).
2. Scan the chapter table for the topic you need.
3. Open the corresponding chapter file for the full detail.

### Writing (a new learning)
1. Decide which topic the new knowledge belongs to.
2. Either:
   - **Existing topic** → open the chapter, add to it. Update the row's
     one-line summary if it shifted.
   - **New topic** → create a new file `chapter-name.md` AND add a new row.
3. Keep the table sorted; pick the next free number.

### Naming
- Lowercase-kebab-case filenames (`aqua-plugin-system.md`).
- One topic per chapter. Split when a chapter exceeds ~300 lines or covers
  two distinct things.

### Granularity rule of thumb
A chapter is right-sized when one paragraph in `MASTER.md` can't capture
what's in it.

---

Mapping of `02 felicias aqua portal work/` and `03 old portal/` codebases.
Synthesised from 6 parallel explore agents.

| 35 | End-customer flow (T1 R5) | [prior research/04-end-customer-flow.md](prior%20research/04-end-customer-flow.md) | T1's Round-5 close of the three-level recursion (Agency → Client → End-customer). `users.ts` storage key for end-customers becomes `email|c:<clientId>` so two clients of the same agency may both have a customer named jane@gmail.com; agency/client tier keep the legacy plain-email key. `getUser`/`verifyPassword`/`setUserPassword`/`updateUser` accept optional `UserLookupScope`. New `POST /api/auth/end-customer/signup` (rate-limited, signupsEnabled gate, 409 on duplicate, issues `lk_session_v1` with `clientId + role=end-customer`). `/api/auth/login` accepts an embed-supplied `clientId` and tries the per-client pool first. `Client.endCustomers: ClientEndCustomerConfig` (`signupsEnabled` default true, optional `postLoginReturnUrl`). `/portal/customer/page.tsx` is variant-driven — looks up website-editor install, calls T3's `getActivePortalVariant` for "account" then "login", renders blocks via `<BlockRenderer>`, falls back to welcome card + customer-panel plugin links. New `/portal/customer/[...rest]` catch-all + `resolveCustomerPluginPage` in the resolver. `PanelId += "customer"`; `buildSidebar` filters by `panelId === "customer"` (or `/portal/customer` href) when scope is `customer`. Embed `LoginForm` carries `clientId` + `allowSignup` + signup toggle + parent-frame return URL (`?return=` or `client.endCustomers.postLoginReturnUrl` or `${origin}/portal/customer`). Smoke green; tsc + build clean. |

ID-token verified via `https://oauth2.googleapis.com/tokeninfo` (Q-ASSUMED for v1; JWKS-local via `jose` deferred to R10). Routes: `GET /api/auth/oauth/google/start?return=<url>` builds the authorize URL + state and 302s; `GET /api/auth/oauth/google/callback` verifies state, exchanges code, looks up `getUser(email)` (no scope — agency/client tier match wins; end-customers go through magic-link), issues `lk_session_v1`, redirects to returnUrl. **First-run bootstrap**: when no agencies registered, OAuth identity bootstraps default "Milesy Media" agency as `agency-owner` (mirrors password-form bootstrap); user row gets a random unguessable password so the password path stays closed for OAuth-bootstrapped accounts (Q-ASSUMED — future round adds `authProviders` set). Unknown email → `redirect(/login?oauth_error=unknown_email)` — the architecture's "contact your agency admin" surface. **Goal B — Magic-link**: `src/lib/server/magicLink.ts`. `signMagicToken({email,clientId,agencyId})` returns token = `base64url(JSON({…,exp,nonce}))`+`.`+HMAC(SHA256, PORTAL_SESSION_SECRET). 15-min TTL; 16-byte random nonce. `verifyMagicToken` rejects malformed/bad-sig/expired/missing-claim. Single-use replay guard via in-memory `Map<nonce,exp>` with on-call GC (v1 limitation: process-local; multi-instance prod needs Redis or `portal_kv` blob — flagged R10). Pluggable delivery via `registerMagicLinkDelivery(fn)`/`deliverMagicLink({…,magicUrl})` returning `{delivered, via:"email-sender"\|"console"}`; T2 R10 registers an adapter at boot so prod magic-link emails go through `EmailService.enqueue()`; until then dev fallback logs the URL. Routes: `POST /api/auth/magic/request` body `{email,clientId,returnUrl?}` resolves clientId → Client, gates on `client.endCustomers.signupsEnabled !== false` (403 — mirrors R5 end-customer-signup gate), per-IP + per-(client,email) rate limits, signs token, calls `deliverMagicLink`. Constant `{ok:true,sent,via}` shape regardless of whether email exists (don't leak account existence). `GET /api/auth/magic/verify?token=…&return=…` verifies, checks `isUsed(nonce)` (replay → `magic_error=already_used`), `markUsed`, looks up or auto-creates the end-customer (token IS proof of email ownership), issues session, redirects. NEW page `/login/magic` server-redirects into `/api/auth/magic/verify` so the user-visible URL stays clean. **Goal C — LoginForm + EmbedLogin**: new props `googleEnabled?`/`magicLinkEnabled?` + new mode `"magic"` alongside `"signin"`/`"signup"`. Magic mode submits to `/api/auth/magic/request`, renders confirmation banner with optional dev click-through. Renders "Continue with Google" `<a>` button + horizontal "or" divider when googleEnabled. "Email me a magic link instead" toggle when `magicLinkEnabled && clientId`. `src/app/login/page.tsx` passes `googleEnabled={isGoogleOAuthConfigured()}` (no clientId at /login → magic hidden); `src/app/embed/login/page.tsx` passes both `googleEnabled` + `magicLinkEnabled={allowSignup}` so end-customers under a Live client get the full passwordless option. **Smoke**: `scripts/smoke-auth-oauth.test.ts` (11 cases) + `scripts/smoke-auth-magic.test.ts` (7 cases) **18/18 pass** via `tsx --test`. OAuth: env gating × 2, authorize-URL shape, state round-trip + bad-sig + malformed reject, `verifyIdToken` happy/audience-mismatch/expired, `exchangeAndVerify` happy + missing-id_token. Magic: round-trip lower-cases email, tampered/malformed/expired reject, single-use mark+replay, delivery hook registered=email-sender + unregistered=console fallback. `npm run smoke:auth-oauth` + `:auth-magic` aliases. tsc clean. **Deviations**: smoke files are `.test.ts` (tsx --test), not `.mjs` — matches T6 R2's `smoke-vercel-domain.test.ts` precedent; tokeninfo not JWKS (Q-ASSUMED); no password-reset (per scope — magic-link covers reset for end-customers, agency-side is future). **Cross-team handoffs**: T2 R10 (email-sender) registers `MagicLinkDelivery` at plugin boot to route emails through EmailService; T6 R2 sets `GOOGLE_OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI` env to `https://<portal-host>/api/auth/oauth/google/callback` in prod (one-line addition to deploy runbook §3 env taxonomy); T3/T4 — no action; T4 polish swaps placeholder `🔐` for the official Google glyph + focus-ring treatment. **R10+ deferred**: shared magic-nonce store (Redis or portal_kv prefix), JWKS-local ID-token verify, `authProviders` field on ServerUser, agency-side password reset, Microsoft/Apple/GitHub OAuth (out of scope per prompt). |

---

## Discipline

- Update this index **before** you finish any task. If a session ends
  without a chapter row, the learning is lost.
- Don't write speculative chapters — only write what's been verified in
  the codebase or confirmed by the user.
- When a chapter goes stale, mark its row with `(stale — superseded by #NN)`
  rather than deleting. The history of decisions matters.
| 66 | Milesy ecosystem — current state snapshot (T4) | [prior research/04-milesy-ecosystem-progress.md](prior%20research/04-milesy-ecosystem-progress.md) | Living document. Single most up-to-date description of T4's BOS + HC build. Three apps under `04-the-final-portal/milesymedia website/` served on unified `:3033`: marketing site (rewritten onto / via portal vercel.json + next.config.ts), `lead magnet app/` (Health Check + shared `hc-questions.js` exposing `window.HC_AREAS`), `business-os app/` (16 pages: index/app/company/leads/trackers/tasks/docs/database/module/marketplace/roadmap/help/request/admin + lessons.js + bos.js). Same-origin localStorage means HC writes `bos.healthCheck` + `bos.leads` and BOS reads them, no cross-port hack. **Funnel**: content → free HC → 🎁 free Business OS (8 niches) → Custom Roadmap (Pro £750) → marketplace add-ons → Aqua agency portal on retainer. **Free-tier sidebar (curated, not exhaustive — Ed's 2026-05-07 ruling)**: My business (Home, About my business) · Learn (Lessons, Health check) · Get help (Need help?, Ask Aqua AI, Book a free call, Request a feature) · More (Custom roadmap Pro, Aqua agency portal locked). **Pro mode** unlocks: My customers (leads kanban) · My numbers (KPIs + time tracker + connectors) · My to-dos (kanban) · My files (SOPs/templates). Free users hitting Pro pages directly see clean lockup with Request-access + Marketplace CTAs. **5 fully-written lessons**: chrome-profile · core-principles · super-sales · ops-sustainability · referral-alchemy (rest visible-but-locked w/ Pro tag). **Marketplace**: 9 add-ons (Inbox, Website Editor, Ecommerce, Fulfilment, Memberships, Affiliates, CRM, Marketing Suite, Finance) all mailto-stub today. **Branding personalisation**: logo file upload (1MB FileReader→data URL) + colour pickers + company name; first-visit modal + re-openable "Customise" button. **Aqua AI floating widget**: 5 free messages, niche+HC-aware mocked replies. **Gamification (slim)**: XP/level/streak/time-saved/achievements, slim home progress strip only after first XP. **Admin**: password gate (`milesy`/`aqua`) + Overview/Leads/Reports/Questions-editor tabs (tree editor area→tier→steps drives live HC via `bos.hcQuestions` override). **Dev**: `python3 -m http.server 3033` from `milesymedia website/` parent (log `/tmp/unified-3033.log`). Cross-refs: chapters 67/68/69/70/71. |

| 68 | HC results honesty contract (T4) | [prior research/04-hc-results-honesty.md](prior%20research/04-hc-results-honesty.md) | Triggered by Ed 2026-05-07 ("make the results not be bs … you've not pulled from google trends or search console so how do you know anything? the data must be real"). Every number on HC results is now either derived honestly from actual answers or marked unknown (`—`) with hint. **No-data state**: skip-to-results without answering anything → "We don't know enough about you yet" headline, all leak cards `—`, transparency block hidden. **Money is range not point**: `headroom × confidence × £1500-£5000` rounded to £100 step. Less coverage = narrower/smaller claim, not padded. If both bounds 0 → "You're ahead of most of the businesses we audit." **Per-topic leak cards** only fill when corresponding topic was answered (`seo`, `site`, `flow`); skipped topics show `—` with "Answer the X topic to fill this" hint. **Sub-headline explicit**: "These are self-reported answers, not pulled from your live data." **Transparency block (always visible when there's data)**: 🧮 "How we got this number" expander explaining headroom/confidence/sector benchmark, 🔌 "What we'd verify against — for the real version" listing 6 connector cards (Search Console / GMB Insights / Lighthouse / GA4 / Stripe·QuickBooks / SERP rank tracker DataForSEO·Ahrefs) linking to marketplace. **Not done**: real connectors not wired (Lighthouse via PageSpeed Insights API would be cheapest first — free, no OAuth); quick-win blog URLs are placeholder slugs at `milesymedia.co/blog/...` that don't exist yet. |

| 72 | AI image editing — variations + inpaint (T3 R005) | [prior research/04-ai-image-editing.md](prior%20research/04-ai-image-editing.md) | T3 R005 closes the AI loop for visual edits. Two new endpoints + two editor modals on top of R9's `imageService`. **Service**: `ImageProviderPort` extended with optional `variations()` + `inpaint()`; `stubImageProvider` implements both — variations derive 4 picsum URLs from `hash(sourceUrl + strength + i)` (deterministic per-source variant set) at 1024×1024; inpaint stub returns the source URL unchanged with `stub: true`. `ImageService.variations({ sourceImageUrl, count?=4, strength? })` consults `monthlyImageCeiling` (each variation = 1), bumps usage on success, raises `CeilingReachedError` over budget. `ImageService.inpaint({ sourceImageUrl, mask, prompt })` = 1 image. Real OpenAI variations / image-edits provider impls deferred — port shape only. **API**: `POST /api/portal/ai-builder/image/variations` body `{ sourceImageUrl, count?, strength? }` → `{ ok, images }` 200 | 429 ceiling-reached. `POST /api/portal/ai-builder/image/inpaint` body `{ sourceImageUrl, mask, prompt }` → `{ ok, image }` 200 | 400 missing args | 429 ceiling. **Editor UI**: `EditorPropertiesSidebar.tsx` grows an "AI tools" sub-section when `selected.type === "image-src"` + draft URL set — two buttons. NEW `ImageVariationsModal.tsx` auto-fires on mount, 2×2 thumbs grid, click "Use this" feeds `handleChange` (existing iframe-patch flow), Regenerate re-rolls. NEW `ImageInpaintModal.tsx` 512×384 canvas overlaying source image, white-on-transparent strokes (radius 18px), prompt textarea, `toDataURL("image/png")` mask serialization, stub-flag surfaces honest "configure OpenAI key for real edits" hint, Clear-mask + Cancel + Generate. Both modals close-loop via the existing patch flow so single-source-of-truth iframe state is preserved. **Smoke**: 6 new tests (variations stub, variations ceiling, inpaint stub, inpaint ceiling, handler shapes 200/400, handler 429). `@aqua/plugin-ai-builder` 14/14 pass. ai-builder + website-editor both tsc-clean. **Files**: `imageService.ts` patch (port + service methods + stub impls); `handlers.ts` patch (`imageVariationsHandler` + `imageInpaintHandler`); `routes.ts` patch (2 new POST routes); `__smoke__/ai-builder.test.ts` patch (+6); `EditorPropertiesSidebar.tsx` patch (AI-tools section + modal mounts); `ImageVariationsModal.tsx` (NEW); `ImageInpaintModal.tsx` (NEW). **Q-ASSUMED**: variations stub fixed at 1024×1024 (real provider impls choose own sizing); inpaint canvas 512×384 (small enough to keep base64 PNG payload manageable); AI-tools sub-section only renders with non-empty draft URL. **R+1 candidates**: real OpenAI image-variations / image-edits provider impl, brush-size + colour controls + eraser tool, history strip of recent variations stored against the image block, side-by-side before/after preview in inpaint modal. |

| 80 | Cookie consent + force-password-change (T3 R007) | [prior research/04-cookie-consent-and-password-change.md](prior%20research/04-cookie-consent-and-password-change.md) | T3 R007 ships two lift-inventory wins from chapter #58 Tier 3. **Goal A — `cookie-consent` storefront block**: NEW `CookieConsentBlock.tsx` registered in `blockRegistry` with 🍪 icon under `content` category. Props `{ message, acceptLabel, declineLabel?, policyUrl?, position: "bottom-bar"|"corner"|"modal" }`. Reads/writes localStorage `aqua_cookie_consent_v1` (exported `COOKIE_CONSENT_KEY`); renders only when no decision on file. Accept/decline dispatches `CustomEvent("aqua-cookie-consent", { detail: { value } })` on `window` so plugins (analytics) can subscribe — accept → fire, decline → suppress. 3 layouts: bottom-bar (full-width strip), corner (360px card bottom-right), modal (centred over 55% scrim). Single-binary v1 — granular categories deferred via versioned key for clean v2 migration. NOT auto-injected into `pageTemplates` (operator-picks-it-up beats every-new-site-grows-a-banner). **Goal B — Force-password-change registry**: NEW `server/forcePasswordChange.ts` — `getRequirePasswordChange(storage, agencyId, userId)` true if per-user flag *or* agency-wide `_all` flag, `setRequirePasswordChange / clearRequirePasswordChange` (per-user `{ setBy, setAt }` records under `t/<agencyId>/_agency/website-editor/force-password/<userId>`), `setRequirePasswordChangeForAgency / clearRequirePasswordChangeForAgency` ("force on all next-login" via `_all` sentinel), `listRequirePasswordChangeUsers` excludes `_all`. Contract documented in chapter §3 — foundation post-auth hook reads `getRequirePasswordChange` and redirects to `/account/change-password`; the password-change handler calls `clearRequirePasswordChange`. Agency-wide `_all` flag is honoured but not auto-cleared per-user after a successful change (failure mode = redirect triggers again, the safer one). Editor admin UI surfacing the toggle next to T1's user-detail page is also out-of-scope — pure registry + handlers ready for T1 to mount. **Smoke**: NEW `__smoke__/r007-cookie-force-password.test.ts` 29/29 — block registration shape + per-user round-trip + agency-wide flag (implies required for any user, scoped to agency, excluded from list) + HTTP shape (GET roster + ?userId, POST per-user true/false, POST agency-wide, 400 paths). package.json test chain extended. website-editor tsc-clean. **Files**: `components/blocks/CookieConsentBlock.tsx` (NEW) · `components/blockRegistry.ts` patch · `server/forcePasswordChange.ts` (NEW) · `api/handlers/forcePassword.ts` (NEW) · `api/routes.ts` patch (2 new routes) · `__smoke__/r007-cookie-force-password.test.ts` (NEW) · `package.json` test-script patch. **R+1 candidates**: granular cookie consent categories (analytics/marketing/strict/preferences) + manage-prefs UX, auto-inject cookie-consent into new-site `pageTemplates` with editor-settings toggle, per-user `lastChanged` timestamp so agency-wide `_all` flag falls off naturally, T1 foundation post-auth redirect hook + `/account/change-password` page, editor admin UI surfacing the toggle in T1's user-detail view. |
| 85 | Storefront blog admin (T3 R008) | [prior research/04-blog-admin.md](prior%20research/04-blog-admin.md) | T3 R008 ships the lift-inventory blog domain inside `@aqua/plugin-website-editor`. **Domain**: NEW `server/blog.ts` — `BlogPost { id, agencyId, clientId, siteId, title, slug, body: Block[], excerpt?, coverImg?, tags[], author?, status: "draft"|"published"|"archived", publishedAt?, createdAt, updatedAt }`. Body is BlockTree (richer than 02 portal's HTML). Per-site CRUD scoped by `(agencyId, clientId, siteId)`. Storage: `t/<a>/<c>/blog/<siteId>/index` (id list newest-first), `t/<a>/<c>/blog/<siteId>/<postId>` (record), `t/<a>/<c>/blog/<siteId>/_slug-index` (slug→id sidecar so `/blog/[slug]` is O(1)). API surface: `createBlogPost / getBlogPost / getBlogPostBySlug / listBlogPosts(filter) / updateBlogPost / deleteBlogPost`. Slug uniqueness on create: auto-disambiguates `-2`/`-3`/… so the call always succeeds. Slug uniqueness on update: throws `BlogSlugConflictError` so operator gets clear error rather than silent renumber. `draft → published` stamps `publishedAt`; subsequent edits keep the original timestamp (SEO-stable). Default `listBlogPosts` excludes archived; `status:"all"` includes them. Sort: published first by publishedAt desc, then drafts by updatedAt desc. **API**: 6 new routes — `GET /blog/posts` (admin/list with `siteId/status/tag/q/limit`), `GET /blog/posts/get?id=…`, `GET /blog/posts/by-slug?slug=…` (returns 404 on archived — storefront gate), `POST /blog/posts` (201 on success, 400 missing siteId or title), `PATCH /blog/posts?siteId=…&id=…` (200 / 404 / 409 slug conflict), `DELETE /blog/posts?siteId=…&id=…` (200 / 404). All gated through `requireClientScope(ctx)`. **Storefront blocks**: NEW `BlogFeedBlock.tsx` (`blog-feed`, 📰, content) — props `{ count=6, layout: "grid"|"list", filterTag?, linkBase="/blog", siteId? }`; auto-fetches `?status=published`; renders cards (cover/title/excerpt/tag chips/N-min-read derived from excerpt at 250 wpm — body-walk R+1); empty/loading/error states inline. NEW `BlogPostBlock.tsx` (`blog-post`, 📄, content) — props `{ slug="auto", siteId? }`; `auto` reads last URL segment so `/blog/[slug]` Just Works; fetches via `/blog/posts/by-slug` (gets 404 on archived); body renders via host-injected `window.__aquaRenderBlocks` if present, else JSON dump (debug-only fallback — production host always injects); header surfaces tags/title/author+date/excerpt lead-in/cover image. Both registered in `blockRegistry`. **Sitemap**: deliberately NOT auto-creating `/blog` + `/blog/[slug]` route templates — host page wires the two blocks manually so operators who don't want a blog aren't forced to delete two pages per new site. **Smoke**: NEW `__smoke__/r008-blog.test.ts` 49/49 pass — block registration (defaults, fields), server CRUD (id shape, slug derivation, auto-disambiguation, explicit slug, publishedAt on status=published, by-slug round-trip + null on miss), list filters (default-excludes-archived, status, tag, query, limit, sort order), status transitions (draft→published stamps publishedAt, published→archived honoured), slug change (slugify normalisation, old slug freed, new routes correctly, conflict throws), delete + slug-index cleanup, HTTP shape (POST 201/400, GET list 200, GET by-slug 200/404, PATCH 200/404/409, DELETE 200/404, by-slug archived → 404 from handler, admin status=all surfaces archived). package.json test chain extended. website-editor tsc-clean. **Files**: `server/blog.ts` (NEW) · `server/storage-keys.ts` patch (3 new keys) · `api/handlers/blog.ts` (NEW) · `api/routes.ts` patch (6 routes) · `components/blocks/BlogFeedBlock.tsx` (NEW) · `components/blocks/BlogPostBlock.tsx` (NEW) · `components/blockRegistry.ts` patch (2 imports + 2 entries) · `__smoke__/r008-blog.test.ts` (NEW) · `package.json` test chain. **Q-ASSUMED**: BlockTree body not HTML; read-time excerpt-derived at 250 wpm (body-walk R+1); admin pages `BlogPostListPage`/`BlogPostEditPage` deferred — operators drive end-to-end via API today, glue is R+1; RSS feed deferred per prompt; archived posts gated 404 from public by-slug, admin sees via `?id=` or `status=all`. **R+1 candidates**: admin list/edit pages mounted on existing editor visual, auto-inject `/blog` + `/blog/[slug]` route templates (toggleable via editor-settings), RSS feed at `/blog/rss.xml`, comments/Disqus, multi-author permissions, body-walk for accurate read-time, scheduled posts (status `scheduled` + `scheduledFor` — domain shape already absorbs it). |

| 76 | `@aqua/plugin-notifications` (T2 R005) | [prior research/04-plugin-notifications.md](prior%20research/04-plugin-notifications.md) | Lifts "notification channels" from chapter #58 Tier 4 lift-inventory; pairs with R003 activity-inbox + R10 email-sender (graceful when either absent — soft requires only). **Shape**: `id:"notifications"`, `scopePolicy:"agency"`, `core:false`. **Domain**: `NotificationRule { id, userId, eventCategories: ActivityCategory[] (empty=all), channels: ChannelKey[] (≥1), cooldownSeconds?, clientIds?: ClientId[] (empty=all), enabled }`. `ChannelKey = email\|slack\|whatsapp\|webhook`. `ChannelConfig` per agency: slack.webhookUrl · whatsapp.{provider, accountSid, fromNumber} · webhook.{url, secretHeaderName, secret} · email.fromAddress. **Storage**: `rules/index` · `rules/by-id/<id>` · `config` · `cooldowns/<userId>/<eventId>` (last-dispatch ts). **Engine** `onActivityEvent(event)` — for each enabled rule whose category+clientId filters match, for each channel: check cooldown → suppress + emit `dispatch.suppressed`, OR call driver + emit `dispatch.{sent\|skipped\|error}`. Returns `MatchedDispatch[]` so callers (UI/smoke) can inspect without subscribing to event bus. **Channel drivers (pluggable ports)**: bundled defaults — emailDriver (uses optional EmailSenderPort + UserPort.getUser; skips with `email_sender_not_installed`/`user_has_no_email` when absent) · slackDriver (POST `{ text }` to webhook; skips on missing URL; errors on HTTP non-2xx) · whatsappDriver (v1 STUB returning `skipped:whatsapp_driver_stub` when configured, `skipped:whatsapp_not_configured` otherwise — full Twilio/Meta-Cloud driver R+1) · webhookDriver (POST `{ subject, body, eventId, metadata }` with optional shared-secret header). | 77 | `@aqua/plugin-bookings` (T2 R006) | [prior research/04-plugin-bookings.md](prior%20research/04-plugin-bookings.md) | Lifts high-value "reservations/bookings" from chapter #58 Tier-1 lift-inventory revival list — Aqua's audience is therapists; therapists book appointments. Per-client booking surface for every Live-phase client. **Shape**: `id:"bookings"`, `scopePolicy:"client"`, `core:false`, soft-pairs with `@aqua/plugin-email-sender` (R10) + `@aqua/plugin-client-crm` (R+1) — graceful when absent. **Domain**: `Service { id, label, durationMin, priceCents?, capacity≥1 (default 1), bufferMin≥0 (default 0), color?, active }` · `Availability { weekdayPattern: { 0..6 → AvailabilityWindow[] }, exceptions: ["YYYY-MM-DD"] }` · `Booking { id, serviceId, startAt, endAt, status: tentative\|confirmed\|cancelled\|completed\|no-show, endCustomerEmail (normalised lowercased), endCustomerName, notes? }`. `STATUS_TRANSITIONS` enforces lifecycle: tentative→confirmed\|cancelled · confirmed→completed\|cancelled\|no-show · cancelled/completed terminal · no-show→confirmed (operator markup). **Slot generator** walks day-by-day, skips `exceptions`, strides `max(1m, durationMin)` across `weekdayPattern[wd]` windows; checks occupying bookings (status ∈ {tentative,confirmed}) — capacity 1 = any time-overlap (extended by `bufferMin` on both sides) blocks; capacity > 1 = same-start consumes one seat, non-aligned overlap blocks entirely. Returns `{ startAt, endAt, remainingCapacity }`. **Buffer carves both sides**: 60m booking @10:00 with 30m buffer blocks [09:30,11:30) → 09:00, 10:00, 11:00 slots all gone (test 5 verifies 8→5). **createBooking idempotent** on `(serviceId, startAt, endCustomerEmail)` with email lowercased+trimmed before compare; non-terminal duplicate returns `{ booking, deduped: true }` rather than fresh row → safe to retry network-flaky storefront submits. Conflict throws `BookingConflictError` (HTTP 409 in handler). **Email + ICS**: `maybeSendConfirmation` builds RFC-5545 ICS via `buildICS()` (folds 75 octets, escapes `;,\n`, minimal VEVENT — no recurrence/method=REQUEST in v1) and calls `emailSender.send({ ..., attachments: [invite.ics] })`. Failures swallowed — downstream email fault must not roll back booking. **CRM merge on completion**: `transition(actor, id, "completed")` calls `crm.mergeFromBooking({ agencyId, clientId, email, name, bookingId })` when port present. **API** (10 routes): services CRUD (4) + availability GET/PATCH (2) + slots GET (public) + bookings list/create/transition (create is public for the storefront block). **Pages**: BookingsCalendarPage (7-column week grid w/ prev/next nav, color/strikethrough by status) · ServicesPage (table + new-service form) · AvailabilityPage (read-only weekly grid; rich editor R+1). **Storefront block**: `booking-form` registered via R5 cross-plugin renderer pattern — picks service → day → slot → submit. **Smoke 12/12**: service CRUD round-trip / create rejects empty label + non-positive duration / setAvailability rejects malformed HH:MM / slot gen respects weekday windows + exceptions (weekend 0; exceptions zero a day) / slot gen respects buffer (8→5 blocked sides) / capacity > 1 group session shares start + remainingCapacity decrements + slot full rejects / createBooking idempotent on (serviceId, startAt, email) with case-only email diffs / createBooking rejects taken slot capacity 1 with BookingConflictError / status transitions follow STATUS_TRANSITIONS happy path + invalid completed→cancelled throws / completed merges to CRM via mergeFromBooking when port present (verifies email/name/bookingId shape) / createBooking enqueues confirmation email with `invite.ics` attachment + `BEGIN:VCALENDAR` body when emailSender installed (no throw when absent) / ICS builder folds long lines + escapes `;,\\\n` + RFC-5545 minimum fields. Empty state renders a chapter-#68-honesty paragraph + `Connect billing →` link — no fabricated MRR when no data. Math: `monthsAgo = (now.year-paid.year)*12 + (now.month-paid.month)` accrued into `buckets[11-monthsAgo]`. (3) **Invoices table** — `GET /api/portal/agency-finance/invoices?clientId=` on mount; populated table (number · issued · due · total · status pill); empty state surfaces `Connect billing → Open agency-finance` CTA; plugin-missing path uses same empty layout with different copy. **Manual invoice quick-add**: `+ Manual invoice` toggles inline form (number + amount £ + due date + status select); POSTs `/invoices` with single-line-item payload (`unitPriceCents=subtotalCents=totalCents=round(amount*100)`, taxCents=0, currency="GBP", dueAt parsed-or-default-14d) + refreshes table. Money formatter handles GBP/USD/EUR symbol prefix; falls back to ISO code. **Wire-up**: per-client `page.tsx` `tab === "finance"` block keeps R7 `<RequirePermission requires={["finance.view"]}>` wrapper; inner placeholder section replaced with `<FinanceTabClient clientId initial={{planTier, lockInPaid, stripeLink}}>`. **Smoke** `§ Finance tab` (5): tab 200 + `client-finance-tab` testid + Plan header + 12-month paid total strip + `invoices?clientId=` 200. tsc clean. HARD BOUNDARY honoured. NOT in scope: real Stripe sync (T6 prod gate), multi-currency, per-invoice line-item editor, auto-overdue computation, editing/deleting invoices from this tab. Q-ASSUMED: GBP default (Aqua UK-based, £100 lock-in); server gates manual-invoice POST on AGENCY_ADMINS so no double-gate on `finance.edit`; sparkline is paid-only (honest "12-month paid total" label, not strict MRR); plugin-missing path = empty-state CTA not deeper degraded mode; reuses `metadata.stripeLink` from R002 reskin (prompt's `stripeUrl` alias kept as synonym in chapter). |
